Many principal works have modern editions in the two series, Corpus Scriptorum Ecclesiasticorum Latinorum and Corpus 
Christianorum. 

For a high proportion English translations exist, such as in the Oxford Library of the Fathers (1838โ81), a series edited by M. 
Dods (T. & T. Clark, and Eerdmans), and three recent series, Library of Christian Classics, Fathers of the Church, and Ancient
